### Modifier management ###
### life_expectancy_modifier ###
DI_add_modifier_life_expectancy_modifier = {
    scope = character
    
    effect = {
        save_scope_as = target
        apply_modifier_effect = {
            MODIFIER_ACTION = add
            MODIFIER_NAME = life_expectancy_modifier
        }
    }
}

DI_remove_modifier_life_expectancy_modifier = {
    scope = character
    
    effect = {
        save_scope_as = target
        apply_modifier_effect = {
            MODIFIER_ACTION = remove
            MODIFIER_NAME = life_expectancy_modifier
        }
    }
}

DI_add_modifier_life_expectancy_modifier_neg = {
    scope = character
    
    effect = {
        save_scope_as = target
        apply_modifier_effect = {
            MODIFIER_ACTION = add
            MODIFIER_NAME = life_expectancy_modifier_neg
        }
    }
}

DI_remove_modifier_life_expectancy_modifier_neg = {
    scope = character
    
    effect = {
        save_scope_as = target
        apply_modifier_effect = {
            MODIFIER_ACTION = remove
            MODIFIER_NAME = life_expectancy_modifier_neg
        }
    }
}

    scope = character

    effect = {
        save_scope_as = target
        apply_modifier_effect = {
            MODIFIER_ACTION = add
            MODIFIER_NAME = heavy_infantry_screen_add
        }
    }
}


DI_remove_modifier_heavy_infantry_screen_add = {
    scope = character

    effect = {
        save_scope_as = target
        apply_modifier_effect = {
            MODIFIER_ACTION = remove
            MODIFIER_NAME = heavy_infantry_screen_add
        }
    }
}

### Clear all Modifiers ###
DI_clear_modifiers = {
    scope = character

    effect = {
        DI_remove_all_character_modifiers_effect = yes
    }
}
